This is the data file for AD&D.  This consists of creatures and treasure from the PH, DMG, MM, MM2, FF, & UA.
Below are the codes used for the creatures' terrain types...

DG = Dungeon
PF = Forest
PH = Hills
PM = Mountains
PP = Plains
PS = Swamp
PD = Desert
FW = Freshwater
SW = Sea
CF = Snowy Forest
CH = Snowy Hills
CM = Snowy Mountains
CP = Snowy Plains
TF = Jungle/Tropics Forest
TH = Jungle/Tropics Hills
TM = Jungle/Tropics Mountains
TS = Jungle/Tropics Swamp
